 1

 donon hi paper main abjective tip sawaal (multiple chwwis queshchan) puche jate hai:paper I:200 ankon ke is paper main rashtriya or antarrashtriya karant afares, bhartiya itihaas or bhartiya rashtriya andolan, bharat or vishwa kaa bhugol, bhartiya rajtantr or gavarnence (samvidhan, political system, panchayat raaj, public policy), aarthik or saamaajik vikaas (sasteneble deveopment, garibi, jansankhya), invyremental ichology, baio-diaversity, climet change or general science jaise vishyon se objective sawaal puche jate hai
 The time limit for adopting this paper is 2 hours
 paper II:200 ank ke is paper main comprihension, interpersonal skills, logical rijning or analitical ability, disijan mekking or problem solving, general mental ability, basic newmaresi or data interpritesan (chart, graph, teble) se sambandhit sawaal puche jate hai
 The time limit for adopting this paper is 2 hours
